      样式冲突
     </strong>
     ：用
     <code>
      &lt;style scoped&gt;
     </code>
     避免组件样式污染全局。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_792">
     </a>
     <strong>
      总结
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      组件是 Vue 的核心
     </strong>
     ，像积木一样拼装页面。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      关键三步
     </strong>
     ：创建组件 → 注册组件 → 使用组件。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      通信方式
     </strong>
     ：父传子用
     <code>
      props
     </code>
     ，子传父用
     <code>
      $emit
     </code>
     。
    </p>
    <h2>
     <a id="06__797">
     </a>
     06 父子组件通信
    </h2>
    <p>
     在 Vue 中，
     <strong>
      父子组件通信
     </strong>
     是最常见的场景，比如父组件传递数据给子组件（如参数），或者子组件通知父组件发生了某些事件（如按钮点击）。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_props_802">
     </a>
     <strong>
      一、父传子：通过
      <code>
       props
      </code>
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__803">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 核心机制
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      父组件
     </strong>
     通过
     <strong>
      属性（props）
     </strong>
     向子组件传递数据。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      子组件
     </strong>
     需要声明接收的
     <code>
      props
     </code>
     ，类似接收快递包裹。
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__807">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 代码示例
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 父组件 Parent.vue --&gt;
&lt;template&gt;
  &lt;div&gt;
    &lt;!-- 传递静态值或动态绑定 --&gt;
    &lt;ChildComponent :message="parentMessage" :count="100" /&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/template&gt;

&lt;script&gt;
import ChildComponent from './Child.vue';

export default {
  components: { ChildComponent },
  data() {
    return {
      parentMessage: "Hello from Parent!"
    };
  }
};
&lt;/script&gt;
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 子组件 Child.vue --&gt;
&lt;template&gt;
  &lt;div&gt;
    &lt;!-- 使用 props --&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;父组件消息：{<!-- -->{ message }}&lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;父组件给的数字：{<!-- -->{ count }}&lt;/p&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/template&gt;

&lt;script&gt;
export default {
  // 声明接收的 props（推荐用对象形式指定类型和默认值）
  props: {
    message: {
      type: String,    // 类型校验
      required: true   // 必传
    },
    count: {
      type: Number,
      default: 0       // 默认值
    }
  }
};
&lt;/script&gt;
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="3__858">
     </a>
     <strong>
      3. 注意事项
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      单向数据流
     </strong>
     ：子组件不能直接修改
     <code>
      props
     </code>
     （否则会警告），若需要修改，应在子组件中用
     <code>
      data
     </code>
     或
     <code>
      computed
     </code>
     接收。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      动态传递
     </strong>
     ：用
     <code>
      v-bind
     </code>
     （或简写
     <code>
      :
     </code>
     ）传递动态数据，如
     <code>
      :count="parentCount"
     </code>
     。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_emit_864">
     </a>
     <strong>
      二、子传父：通过
      <code>
       $emit
      </code>
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__865">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 核心机制
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      子组件
     </strong>
     通过
     <code>
      $emit
     </code>
     <strong>
      触发自定义事件
     </strong>
     ，类似打电话通知父组件。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      父组件
     </strong>
     通过
     <code>
      v-on
     </code>
     （或简写
     <code>
      @
     </code>
     ）
     <strong>
      监听事件
     </strong>
     并处理。
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__869">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 代码示例
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 子组件 Child.vue --&gt;
&lt;template&gt;
  &lt;button @click="handleClick"&gt;点我通知父组件&lt;/button&gt;
&lt;/template&gt;

&lt;script&gt;
export default {
  methods: {
    handleClick() {
      // 触发自定义事件，并传递数据
      this.$emit('child-click', { data: "子组件的数据" });
    }
  }
};
&lt;/script&gt;
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 父组件 Parent.vue --&gt;
&lt;template&gt;
  &lt;div&gt;
    &lt;!-- 监听子组件触发的事件 --&gt;
    &lt;ChildComponent @child-click="handleChildClick" /&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/template&gt;

&lt;script&gt;
import ChildComponent from './Child.vue';

export default {
  components: { ChildComponent },
  methods: {
    // 接收子组件传递的数据
    handleChildClick(payload) {
      console.log("收到子组件的消息：", payload.data); // 输出：收到子组件的消息：子组件的数据
    }
  }
};
&lt;/script&gt;
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="3__912">
     </a>
     <strong>
      3. 注意事项
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      事件命名
     </strong>
     ：推荐使用
     <strong>
      kebab-case
     </strong>
     （如
     <code>
      child-click
     </code>
     ），因为 HTML 不区分大小写。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      参数传递
     </strong>
     ：
     <code>
      $emit
     </code>
     的第二个参数可以是任意类型数据（如对象、数组）。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="vmodel__sync_918">
     </a>
     <strong>
      三、简化写法：
      <code>
       v-model
      </code>
      与
      <code>
       .sync
      </code>
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_vmodel_919">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1.
      <code>
       v-model
      </code>
      （双向绑定简化版）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     • 适用于表单类组件，如自定义输入框。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      本质
     </strong>
     ：是
     <code>
      :value
     </code>
     +
     <code>
      @input
     </code>
     的语法糖。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 父组件 --&gt;
&lt;ChildComponent v-model="parentValue" /&gt;

&lt;!-- 等价于 --&gt;
&lt;ChildComponent :value="parentValue" @input="parentValue = $event" /&gt;
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 子组件 --&gt;
&lt;template&gt;
  &lt;input :value="value" @input="$emit('input', $event.target.value)" /&gt;
&lt;/template&gt;

&lt;script&gt;
export default {
  props: ['value']  // 必须接收名为 value 的 prop
};
&lt;/script&gt;
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2_sync__944">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2.
      <code>
       .sync
      </code>
      修饰符
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     • 用于简化父子组件间的“双向绑定”（Vue 2.3+ 支持）。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      本质
     </strong>
     ：是
     <code>
      :propName
     </code>
     +
     <code>
      @update:propName
     </code>
     的语法糖。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 父组件 --&gt;
&lt;ChildComponent :title.sync="parentTitle" /&gt;

&lt;!-- 等价于 --&gt;
&lt;ChildComponent :title="parentTitle" @update:title="parentTitle = $event" /&gt;
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;!-- 子组件 --&gt;
&lt;button @click="$emit('update:title', '新标题')"&gt;修改标题&lt;/button&gt;
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_963">
     </a>
     <strong>
      四、父子通信示意图
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <pre><code>父组件 → 子组件：通过 props（单向）
子组件 → 父组件：通过 $emit 事件（触发父组件方法）
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_971">
     </a>
     <strong>
      五、常见问题
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__props_972">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 为什么子组件不能直接修改 props？
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     • 为了遵循
     <strong>
      单向数据流
     </strong>
     ，保证数据来源清晰可追踪。若需要修改，应该：
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      子组件内部
     </strong>
     用
     <code>
      data
     </code>
     接收 props 的初始值：
     <br/>
     <code>
      javascript data() { return { localData: this.parentData }; }
     </code>
     <br/>
     • 或通过
     <code>
      $emit
     </code>
     让父组件修改原始数据。
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__982">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 如何传递复杂数据（如对象、数组）？
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     • 直接传递即可，Vue 会自动检测对象内部变化（需注意引用类型的特性）。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_987">
     </a>
     <strong>
      总结
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      父传子
     </strong>
     ：用
     <code>
      props
     </code>
     ，子组件声明接收。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      子传父
     </strong>
     ：用
     <code>
      $emit
     </code>
     ，父组件监听事件。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      简化双向绑定
     </strong>
     ：
     <code>
      v-model
     </code>
     用于表单，
     <code>
      .sync
     </code>
     用于其他场景。
     <br/>
     • 保持数据流的清晰性，是 Vue 组件化开发的关键！
    </p>
    <h2>
     <a id="07_axios_993">
     </a>
     07 axios
    </h2>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Axios
     </strong>
     是一个基于 Promise 的 HTTP 客户端库，专门用于浏览器和 Node.js 中发送 HTTP 请求。它简单易用，支持异步请求、拦截请求和响应、自动转换 JSON 数据等功能，是前端开发中与后端 API 交互的常用工具。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="Axios__998">
     </a>
     <strong>
      一、Axios 的核心优势
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <strong>
       简单语法
      </strong>
      ：链式调用，类似
      <code>
       fetch
      </code>
      但更简洁。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       自动转换数据
      </strong>
      ：自动将响应数据解析为 JSON，无需手动处理。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       拦截器
      </strong>
      ：可以在请求发送前或响应返回后统一处理逻辑（如添加 Token、处理错误）。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       取消请求
      </strong>
      ：支持取消未完成的请求（比如用户频繁点击时）。
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_Axios_1007">
     </a>
     <strong>
      二、安装 Axios
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__npm__1008">
     </a>
     1. 通过 npm 安装（推荐）：
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-bash"><span class="token function">npm</span> <span class="token function">install</span> axios
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__CDN__1013">
     </a>
     2. 通过 CDN 引入：
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-html"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>script</span> <span class="token attr-name">src</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/axios/dist/axios.min.js<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token script"></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>script</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1020">
     </a>
     <strong>
      三、基础用法示例
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__GET__1022">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 发送 GET 请求
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token comment">// 语法：axios.get(url, [配置参数])</span>
axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'https://api.example.com/data'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">then</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">response</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 响应数据</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">catch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">error</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">error</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请求失败:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__POST__1034">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 发送 POST 请求
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token comment">// 语法：axios.post(url, 请求体数据, [配置参数])</span>
axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">post</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'https://api.example.com/users'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'John'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">age</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">30</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">then</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">response</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'创建成功:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">catch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">error</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">error</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'创建失败:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="3_PUTDELETE_1049">
     </a>
     <strong>
      3. 发送其他请求（PUT、DELETE）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token comment">// PUT 请求（更新数据）</span>
axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">put</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'https://api.example.com/users/1'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'Alice'</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token comment">// DELETE 请求（删除数据）</span>
axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">delete</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'https://api.example.com/users/1'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1062">
     </a>
     <strong>
      四、配置参数详解
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     Axios 支持全局配置和请求级别的配置：
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__1065">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 全局默认配置
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript">axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span>defaults<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseURL <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">'https://api.example.com'</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 统一设置根路径</span>
axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span>defaults<span class="token punctuation">.</span>headers<span class="token punctuation">.</span>common<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'Authorization'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">'Bearer token123'</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 统一添加请求头</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__1071">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 单个请求配置
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript">axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/data'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">params</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>          <span class="token comment">// URL 参数（自动转为 ?id=1）</span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">headers</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token string-property property">'X-Custom-Header'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'value'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// 自定义请求头</span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">timeout</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5000</span>               <span class="token comment">// 超时时间（毫秒）</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1082">
     </a>
     <strong>
      五、错误处理
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     Axios 的错误分为两种：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <strong>
       请求成功，但 HTTP 状态码非 2xx
      </strong>
      （如 404、500）。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       请求本身失败
      </strong>
      （如网络错误、跨域问题）。
     </li>
    </ol>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript">axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/data'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">then</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">response</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token comment">// 处理成功响应</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">catch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">error</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>response<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token comment">// 请求已发送，服务器返回了错误状态码（如 404）</span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'状态码:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>status<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'错误数据:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>request<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token comment">// 请求已发送，但未收到响应（如网络断开）</span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'未收到响应:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>request<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token comment">// 其他错误（如配置错误）</span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'错误信息:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>message<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1109">
     </a>
     <strong>
      六、拦截器（高级用法）
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     拦截器可以在请求或响应被处理前统一处理逻辑：
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__1112">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 请求拦截器
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript">axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span>interceptors<span class="token punctuation">.</span>request<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">use</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">config</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token comment">// 在发送请求前添加 Token</span>
  config<span class="token punctuation">.</span>headers<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Authorization <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">'Bearer token123'</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">return</span> config<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token parameter">error</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">return</span> Promise<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reject</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__1123">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 响应拦截器
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript">axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span>interceptors<span class="token punctuation">.</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">use</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">response</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token comment">// 对响应数据统一处理（如提取 data 字段）</span>
  <span class="token keyword">return</span> response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token parameter">error</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token comment">// 统一处理错误</span>
  <span class="token function">alert</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请求失败，请重试！'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">return</span> Promise<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reject</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_Vue__Axios_1137">
     </a>
     <strong>
      七、在 Vue 项目中使用 Axios
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__1138">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 在组件中直接使用
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-vue">&lt;script&gt;
import axios from 'axios';

export default {
  data() {
    return {
      users: []
    };
  },
  created() {
    axios.get('https://api.example.com/users')
      .then(response =&gt; {
        this.users = response.data;
      })
      .catch(error =&gt; {
        console.error(error);
      });
  }
};
&lt;/script&gt;
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__1162">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 全局挂载（推荐）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     在
     <code>
      main.js
     </code>
     中全局引入：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">import</span> axios <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">'axios'</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token comment">// 全局配置</span>
axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span>defaults<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseURL <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">'https://api.example.com'</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token comment">// 挂载到 Vue 原型（Vue2 用法）</span>
<span class="token class-name">Vue</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span>$axios <span class="token operator">=</span> axios<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token comment">// 在组件中直接使用</span>
<span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>$axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/users'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">then</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">...</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1179">
     </a>
     <strong>
      八、常见问题
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_CORS_1180">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 跨域问题（CORS）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     • 跨域是浏览器的安全限制，需后端配置
     <code>
      Access-Control-Allow-Origin
     </code>
     。
     <br/>
     • 开发环境可通过代理解决（如 Vue CLI 的
     <code>
      proxy
     </code>
     配置）。
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__1184">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 处理文件上传
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">const</span> formData <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">FormData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">append</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'file'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> file<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// file 是 input[type=file] 的文件对象</span>

axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">post</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/upload'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">headers</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token string-property property">'Content-Type'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'multipart/form-data'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1196">
     </a>
     <strong>
      总结
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     Axios 是前端与后端交互的利器，掌握它的基本用法和配置，能让你高效处理 HTTP 请求。初学时重点关注：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <strong>
       GET/POST 请求的发送
      </strong>
      。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       错误处理
      </strong>
      （避免程序崩溃）。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       拦截器的简单使用
      </strong>
      （如添加 Token）。
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h2>
     <a id="08_axiosajax_1202">
     </a>
     08 axios和ajax的区别
    </h2>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Axios 和 Ajax 的核心区别
     </strong>
     <br/>
     Axios 和 Ajax 都用于前端与服务器的异步数据交互，但它们在实现方式、功能和使用体验上有显著差异：
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__1210">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 定义与背景
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      Ajax (Asynchronous JavaScript and XML)
     </strong>
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      概念
     </strong>
     ：一种技术统称，基于
     <code>
      XMLHttpRequest
     </code>
     对象实现异步请求，无需刷新页面即可更新数据。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      诞生时间
     </strong>
     ：2005 年（历史悠久，兼容性广泛）。
    </p>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      Axios
     </strong>
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      概念
     </strong>
     ：一个基于 Promise 的
     <strong>
      第三方 HTTP 客户端库
     </strong>
     ，封装了
     <code>
      XMLHttpRequest
     </code>
     ，提供更简洁的 API。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      诞生时间
     </strong>
     ：2014 年后（现代开发常用工具）。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="2__1221">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 核心实现方式
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        <strong>
         特性
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         Ajax
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         Axios
        </strong>
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         底层依赖
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        原生
        <code>
         XMLHttpRequest
        </code>
        对象
       </td>
       <td>
        封装了
        <code>
         XMLHttpRequest
        </code>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         语法风格
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        回调函数（Callback Hell 风险）
       </td>
       <td>
        Promise/Async Await（链式调用，代码更清晰）
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         代码复杂度
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        代码冗长，需手动处理更多细节
       </td>
       <td>
        开箱即用，API 简洁
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         JSON 数据处理
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        需手动解析
        <code>
         JSON.parse()
        </code>
       </td>
       <td>
        自动转换 JSON 数据
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="3__1231">
     </a>
     <strong>
      3. 功能特性对比
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      Ajax 的局限性
     </strong>
     <br/>
     • 需要自行处理跨浏览器兼容性（如旧版 IE）。
     <br/>
     • 需手动设置请求头、转换数据格式。
     <br/>
     • 错误处理分散，易产生回调地狱。
    </p>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      Axios 的优势
     </strong>
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      拦截器
     </strong>
     ：统一处理请求和响应（如添加 Token、日志监控）。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      取消请求
     </strong>
     ：通过
     <code>
      CancelToken
     </code>
     中止未完成的请求。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      并发处理
     </strong>
     ：支持
     <code>
      axios.all()
     </code>
     同时发送多个请求。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      浏览器兼容
     </strong>
     ：自动适配新旧浏览器（包括 IE11）。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="4__1245">
     </a>
     <strong>
      4. 代码示例
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="_Ajax__GET__1246">
     </a>
     <strong>
      原生 Ajax 实现 GET 请求
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">const</span> xhr <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">XMLHttpRequest</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'GET'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'https://api.example.com/data'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">onreadystatechange</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span>readyState <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">4</span> <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span>status <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> data <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token constant">JSON</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">parse</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span>responseText<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 手动解析 JSON</span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>data<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span>status <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">error</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请求失败:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span>status<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
xhr<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">send</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="Axios__GET__1261">
     </a>
     <strong>
      Axios 实现 GET 请求
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript">axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'https://api.example.com/data'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">then</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">response</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 自动解析 JSON</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">catch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">error</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">error</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请求失败:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="5__1274">
     </a>
     <strong>
      5. 错误处理差异
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      Ajax
     </strong>
     ：需在回调中检查
     <code>
      status
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      readyState
     </code>
     ，错误处理分散。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      Axios
     </strong>
     ：通过
     <code>
      .catch()
     </code>
     集中捕获错误，且能区分请求错误和响应错误：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript">axios<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/data'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">catch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">error</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>response<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'服务器返回错误状态码:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>status<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>request<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请求已发送但无响应:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>request<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'配置错误:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>message<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="09__1291">
     </a>
     09 计算属性
    </h2>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1293">
     </a>
     <strong>
      一、计算属性是什么？
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      定义
     </strong>
     ：计算属性是
     <strong>
      基于响应式依赖动态计算的值
     </strong>
     ，它会根据依赖的数据自动更新结果。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      核心特点
     </strong>
     ：
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      缓存机制
     </strong>
     ：依赖的数据未变化时，直接返回缓存值，避免重复计算。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      声明式逻辑
     </strong>
     ：将复杂逻辑封装为属性，模板中可像普通数据一样使用。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      适用场景
     </strong>
     ：
     <br/>
     • 需要根据已有数据动态计算的场景（如：购物车总价、数据过滤）。
     <br/>
     • 模板中需要简化复杂表达式时。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_vs__1304">
     </a>
     <strong>
      二、计算属性 vs 方法
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        <strong>
         对比维度
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         计算属性（Computed）
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         方法（Methods）
        </strong>
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         触发时机
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        依赖数据变化时重新计算
       </td>
       <td>
        每次调用时重新执行
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         缓存
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        有缓存（依赖不变时复用结果）
       </td>
       <td>
        无缓存（每次调用重新计算）
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         模板中使用方式
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        作为属性使用（无需括号）
       </td>
       <td>
        作为方法调用（需括号）
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         性能
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        适合频繁计算的复杂逻辑（高效）
       </td>
       <td>
        适合不频繁或需要参数的场景
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="Vuejs__1314">
     </a>
     <strong>
      三、Vue.js 中的计算属性示例
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__1315">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 基础用法
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">default</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token function">data</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">price</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">quantity</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">computed</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token comment">// 计算总价（依赖 price 和 quantity）</span>
    <span class="token function">total</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>price <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>quantity<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在模板中直接使用：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-html"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>p</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>总价：{<!-- -->{ total }}<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>p</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>  <span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 输出：500 --&gt;</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__1337">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 复杂逻辑封装
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">computed</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token comment">// 过滤出价格大于 50 的商品</span>
  <span class="token function">filteredProducts</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>products<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">filter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">product</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> product<span class="token punctuation">.</span>price <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">50</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1349">
     </a>
     <strong>
      四、计算属性的缓存机制
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      缓存生效条件
     </strong>
     ：只有当依赖的响应式数据（如
     <code>
      price
     </code>
     、
     <code>
      quantity
     </code>
     ）变化时，才会重新计算。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      手动跳过缓存
     </strong>
     ：若需每次都重新计算，应改用
     <strong>
      方法（Methods）
     </strong>
     。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_Setter_1355">
     </a>
     <strong>
      五、计算属性的 Setter（高级用法）
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     计算属性默认只有
     <code>
      getter
     </code>
     ，但也可手动定义
     <code>
      setter
     </code>
     ：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">computed</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">fullName</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>firstName <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">' '</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>lastName<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token function">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>newValue<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token comment">// 当修改 fullName 时，拆分并更新 firstName 和 lastName</span>
      <span class="token keyword">const</span> names <span class="token operator">=</span> newValue<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">split</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>firstName <span class="token operator">=</span> names<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>lastName <span class="token operator">=</span> names<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">''</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     使用示例：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>fullName <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">'John Doe'</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>  <span class="token comment">// 自动触发 setter</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1380">
     </a>
     <strong>
      六、代码实战练习
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token comment">// 示例：根据用户输入过滤列表</span>
<span class="token function">data</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">searchText</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">''</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">products</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
      <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'Apple'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">price</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'Banana'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">price</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'Orange'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">price</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">8</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">]</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
<span class="token literal-property property">computed</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token function">filteredProducts</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>products<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">filter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">product</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> 
      product<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toLowerCase</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">includes</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>searchText<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toLowerCase</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     模板中使用：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-html"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token attr-name">v-model</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>searchText<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">placeholder</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>搜索商品<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>ul</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>li</span> <span class="token attr-name">v-for</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>product in filteredProducts<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">:key</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>product.name<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
    {<!-- -->{ product.name }} - ￥{<!-- -->{ product.price }}
  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>li</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>ul</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="10__1413">
     </a>
     10 监听器
    </h2>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <strong>
      侦听器（Watcher）
     </strong>
     是前端框架（如 Vue.js）中用于监听数据变化并执行特定逻辑的功能，尤其适合处理异步操作或复杂数据变更场景。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1420">
     </a>
     <strong>
      一、侦听器的核心概念
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      作用
     </strong>
     ：监听某个数据的变化，并在变化时触发回调函数。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      适用场景
     </strong>
     ：
     <br/>
     • 数据变化后需执行异步操作（如 API 请求）。
     <br/>
     • 数据变化后需执行复杂逻辑（如多个步骤处理）。
     <br/>
     • 需要观察数据变化的具体过程（如旧值和新值对比）。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="Vuejs__1429">
     </a>
     <strong>
      二、Vue.js 中的侦听器示例
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__1430">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 基础用法
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">default</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token function">data</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">count</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">userInput</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">''</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token comment">// 监听 count 的变化</span>
    <span class="token function">count</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal<span class="token punctuation">,</span> oldVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">count 从 </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>oldVal<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> 变为 </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>newVal<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token comment">// 监听用户输入的变化（用于搜索联想）</span>
    <span class="token function">userInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">fetchSearchResults</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>newVal<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 调用异步方法</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">methods</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token function">fetchSearchResults</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">query</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token comment">// 模拟 API 请求</span>
      <span class="token function">setTimeout</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'搜索:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> query<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">300</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1462">
     </a>
     <strong>
      三、侦听器的配置选项
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     通过对象语法，可配置
     <code>
      handler
     </code>
     函数及监听策略：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">dataToWatch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token function">handler</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal<span class="token punctuation">,</span> oldVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token comment">/* 逻辑 */</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">deep</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>      <span class="token comment">// 深度监听（对象内部变化）</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">immediate</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span>  <span class="token comment">// 立即触发（初始化时执行一次）</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_deep_1474">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 深度监听（deep）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     用于监听对象或数组内部属性的变化：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function">data</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">user</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'Alice'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">age</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">25</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
<span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">user</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token function">handler</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'用户信息变化:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> newVal<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">deep</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token comment">// 监听 user 对象所有属性的变化</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2_immediate_1492">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 立即执行（immediate）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     初始化时立即触发一次侦听逻辑：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">count</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token function">handler</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'初始值:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> newVal<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 初始化时打印 count 的初始值</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">immediate</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1509">
     </a>
     <strong>
      四、经典使用场景
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__1510">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 表单输入实时校验
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token function">email</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">validateEmail</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>newVal<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>error <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">'邮箱格式错误'</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>error <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">''</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__1523">
     </a>
     <strong>
      2. 路由参数变化重新加载数据
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token string">'$route.params.id'</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>newId<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">fetchData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>newId<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 路由变化时重新请求数据</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="3__1532">
     </a>
     <strong>
      3. 监听对象属性变化（需深度监听）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token string-property property">'formData.username'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token function">handler</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'用户名变化:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> newVal<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="11__1545">
     </a>
     11 计算属性和侦听器的区别
    </h2>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <strong>
      计算属性（Computed Properties）与侦听器（Watchers）的区别
     </strong>
    </p>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        <strong>
         对比维度
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         计算属性（Computed）
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         侦听器（Watchers）
        </strong>
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         核心目的
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         动态计算并返回新值
        </strong>
        ，用于模板展示或依赖其他数据的场景。
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         响应数据变化
        </strong>
        ，执行副作用（如异步操作、复杂逻辑）。
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         缓存机制
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         有缓存
        </strong>
        ：依赖数据未变化时直接返回缓存结果，避免重复计算。
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         无缓存
        </strong>
        ：每次数据变化均触发回调。
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         语法定义
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        在
        <code>
         computed
        </code>
        选项中定义，返回计算结果。
       </td>
       <td>
        在
        <code>
         watch
        </code>
        选项中定义，指定监听的数据及回调函数。
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         依赖追踪
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         自动追踪依赖
        </strong>
        ：根据函数内使用的响应式数据自动更新。
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         手动指定依赖
        </strong>
        ：需明确监听特定数据或路径。
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         返回值
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        必须返回一个值，供模板或逻辑使用。
       </td>
       <td>
        无需返回值，侧重执行操作。
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         适用场景
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        1. 模板中需要动态计算的表达式（如拼接字符串、过滤列表）。
        <br/>
        2. 依赖多个数据的同步计算（如购物车总价）。
       </td>
       <td>
        1. 数据变化后需执行异步任务（如API请求）。
        <br/>
        2. 需要旧值和新值对比的场景（如记录变化历史）。
        <br/>
        3. 监听非响应式数据或复杂对象内部变化（需
        <code>
         deep: true
        </code>
        ）。
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <strong>
         性能优化
        </strong>
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         高效
        </strong>
        ：依赖不变时直接使用缓存，适合频繁计算的场景。
       </td>
       <td>
        <strong>
         需谨慎使用
        </strong>
        ：频繁变化的数据可能引发多次回调，需防抖或节流。
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1562">
     </a>
     <strong>
      核心区别解析
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        设计目的不同
       </strong>
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        计算属性
       </strong>
       ：核心是
       <strong>
        派生新数据
       </strong>
       。例如，将
       <code>
        firstName
       </code>
       和
       <code>
        lastName
       </code>
       组合成
       <code>
        fullName
       </code>
       。
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        侦听器
       </strong>
       ：核心是
       <strong>
        观察数据变化后的动作
       </strong>
       。例如，用户输入搜索关键词时自动发起API请求。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        响应方式不同
       </strong>
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        计算属性
       </strong>
       ：自动追踪函数内部依赖的响应式数据，依赖变化时重新计算。
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        侦听器
       </strong>
       ：需手动指定监听的目标数据，且支持深度监听（
       <code>
        deep: true
       </code>
       ）或立即触发（
       <code>
        immediate: true
       </code>
       ）。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        缓存机制的影响
       </strong>
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        计算属性
       </strong>
       ：多次访问同一计算属性时，只要依赖未变化，直接返回缓存值，避免重复计算。
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        侦听器
       </strong>
       ：每次数据变化均触发回调，适合需要实时响应的场景（如输入框校验）。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1578">
     </a>
     <strong>
      何时使用计算属性？
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      场景1
     </strong>
     ：需要基于现有数据动态生成新值。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">computed</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token function">totalPrice</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>items<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reduce</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">sum<span class="token punctuation">,</span> item</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> sum <span class="token operator">+</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span>price<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      场景2
     </strong>
     ：模板中有复杂表达式需简化。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-html"><span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 模板中直接使用计算属性 --&gt;</span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>p</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>{<!-- -->{ fullName }}<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>p</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1595">
     </a>
     <strong>
      何时使用侦听器？
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      场景1
     </strong>
     ：数据变化后需执行异步操作。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token function">searchText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">debouncedFetchResults</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>newVal<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 防抖后请求</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      场景2
     </strong>
     ：需要深度监听对象或数组内部变化。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token literal-property property">watch</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token literal-property property">user</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token function">handler</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">newVal</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      console<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'用户信息变化:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> newVal<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">deep</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token comment">// 监听 user 对象所有属性</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1618">
     </a>
     <strong>
      总结
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      计算属性
     </strong>
     ：用于
     <strong>
      同步计算派生数据
     </strong>
     ，优先使用，提升代码可读性和性能。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      侦听器
     </strong>
     ：用于
     <strong>
      数据变化后的副作用操作
     </strong>
     （如异步、DOM操作），需谨慎避免滥用。
    </p>
    <h2>
     <a id="12__1623">
     </a>
     12 插槽
    </h2>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1626">
     </a>
     <strong>
      插槽是什么？
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     想象你有一个
     <strong>
      手机壳
     </strong>
     ，壳子上预留了摄像头和按钮的孔位。
     <br/>
     <strong>
      插槽
     </strong>
     就像这些孔位——壳子（子组件）定义好结构，你（父组件）可以按需要插入不同的摄像头模组或按钮（自定义内容）。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1632">
     </a>
     <strong>
      为什么需要插槽？
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      插槽
     </strong>
     就是解决这个问题的：
     <strong>
      壳子固定，内容随便换
     </strong>
     ！
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1638">
     </a>
     <strong>
      插槽的三种用法
     </strong>
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__1640">
     </a>
     <strong>
      1. 默认插槽（万能孔）
     </strong>
    </h5>
    <p>
     •
     <strong>
      子组件
     </strong>
     ：预留一个“万能孔”，不指定内容时显示默认值。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-html"><span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 子组件：Card.vue --&gt;</span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token attr-name">class</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>card<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>slot</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>默认提示文字<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>slot</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> <span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 这里是插槽位置 --&gt;</span>
